       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         <i>
          Like everyone else, Jack had grown up hearing stories about what it was like for people to fall in love with their soulmates. The story went that, as soulmates’ feelings for each other grew, the world ignited into color in a way that those who had not found their soulmates would, apparently, never be able to understand.
         </i>
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Kate forgot how awkward and confusing Gibbs can be. Gibbs forgot that Kate doesn't back down from a challenge and is just as curious and stubborn as he is.
        </p>
        <p>
         Neither of them expected to find something they had long wanted hidden in the translation :)
        </p>
        <p>
         ~~~
        </p>
        <p>
         Hover boxes will (in theory - please let me know if any don't work) appear with translation if you move your mouse over the foreign language phrases, however, I did test this on non-linguists ;) and you
         <i>
          don't
         </i>
         need to know exactly what's being said to follow the story ;D You'll just be in the same position as Kate, so whether you choose initially to read it without sneaking a peek or not is up to you.
        </p>
        <p>
         I have also provided translations at the end for people on tablets or mobile phones, for whom the hover boxes won't work.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         She had made her peace with it. They couldn't be together.
         <br/>
         Pete loved her, and she would build a life with him.
        </p>
        <p>
         Until Annie Lennox started playing on the jukebox.
        </p>
        <p>
         Some scenes that should have been in Threads (8-18), and a moment of justice for fellow "ugh"ers of Pete...
        </p>
        <p>
         --oOo--
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         In the months following the Za'tarc test, Sam has replayed her conversation with her C.O. daily.
         <br/>
         She has been true to her word. Nothing that passed between them has ever left the room.
        </p>
        <p>
         No-one has to know that she visits the room every chance she gets.
         <br/>
         And as long as she remembers to shut the door carefully behind her, no-one ever will.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
        </p>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          He bought a house.
         </p>
         <p>
          Or he started the process of buying a house. Sam realizes she doesn't want to know which, as he guides her from one room to the next, chatting incessantly. She follows him in a daze, as if she's walking through waist high water, trying and failing to listen and actually hear what he's saying.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        Or Kerry isn't at Jack's house
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         “Why did you touch the sacred stone?”
         <br/>
         Jack did touch the stone, but in his defence, it looked neat. All round and glittery.
         <br/>
         He shrugged, “It’s who I am as a person.”
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Sam lurches forward, hand raised, and finger pointing at Thor. “No way, I’m gonna let you-”
        </p>
        <p>
         The white light engulfs her.
        </p>
        <p>
         “-sacrifice yourself.” Her feet connect with the wooden top of the General’s desk as he, himself, comes into sight at an unusual angle. The momentum propels her forward. Before she can contemplate her strange situation, she steps on air. “Ahh-”
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Jack’s Mark rolls and twists up over his left bicep and spreads over his heart. The thick, dark ink loops in large circles with smaller, solid circles dotting each ring in no particular pattern. In the middle of the ring, right over his heart, in shining gold lettering against the solid black ink is a solitary S.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         "I thought Thor put preventative measures in place to deter Loki from attempting to clone you again, O'Neill." His face was perfectly straight except for the slight crinkle at his left eye, which only those who knew him well even knew to look for.
        </p>
        <p>
         "Not Loki." the two muttered in tandem.
        </p>
       </blockquote>
